### ðŸ› ï¸ If you want a script...

Hereâ€™s a quick **PowerShell renamer** to fix legacy files and apply that format:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem -Path "." -Filter "Loop_*.md" | ForEach-Object {
    $newName = ($_ -replace '[^0-9]', '').PadLeft(3, '0')
    $title = ($_ -replace '^Loop_\d+_', '') -replace '[^a-zA-Z0-9]', ' '
    $titleCase = -join ($title -split ' ' | ForEach-Object { $_.Substring(0,1).ToUpper() + $_.Substring(1).ToLower() }) -replace '\s+', '_'
    Rename-Item $_ -NewName ("Loop_{0}_{1}.md" -f $newName, $titleCase)
}
```

## ðŸ› ï¸ DROP-IN RENAME SCRIPT (PowerShell)

Hereâ€™s a **plug-and-run PowerShell script** to:
- Fix any existing `Loop_*` filenames
- Normalize the number to 3 digits
- Title-case and underscore the rest

### ðŸ”§ Script:
```powershell
Get-ChildItem -Path "." -Filter "Loop*.md" | ForEach-Object {
    $originalName = $_.BaseName
    if ($originalName -match "^Loop[_-]?(\d{1,3})[_-]?(.*)$") {
        $loopNum = $matches[1].PadLeft(3, '0')
        $titleRaw = $matches[2] -replace '[_\-.]', ' '
        $titleClean = ($titleRaw -split '\s+') | ForEach-Object { 
            if ($_ -ne '') { $_.Substring(0,1).ToUpper() + $_.Substring(1).ToLower() } 
        } -join '_'
        $newName = "Loop_${loopNum}_${titleClean}.md"
        Rename-Item $_.FullName -NewName $newName
        Write-Output "Renamed: $originalName -> $newName"
    }
}
```

### ðŸ’¡ How to use:
1. Save that as `rename-loops.ps1`
2. Place it in your `100s` folder
3. Open **PowerShell** in that folder
4. Run:  
```powershell
.\rename-loops.ps1
```

Get-ChildItem -Path "." -Filter "Loop*.md" | ForEach-Object {
    if ($_.BaseName -match "^Loop[_-]?(\d{1,3})[_-]?(.*)$") {
        $loopNum = $matches[1].PadLeft(3, '0')
        $titleRaw = $matches[2] -replace '[_\-.]', ' '
        $titleClean = ($titleRaw -split '\s+') | ForEach-Object { 
            if ($_ -ne '') { $_.Substring(0,1).ToUpper() + $_.Substring(1).ToLower() } 
        } -join '_'
        $newName = "Loop_${loopNum}_${titleClean}.md"
        Rename-Item $_.FullName -NewName $newName
        Write-Output "âœ… Renamed: $($_.Name) -> $newName"
    }
}
